"/***************************************************************\n"

"            <blockquote>\r\n"

"            </blockquote>\r\n"
"            </p>\r\n"
"\r\n"
"            <p>where \"$CATALINA_HOME\" is the root of the Tomcat installation directory. If y"
"ou're seeing this page, and you don't think you should be, then either you're either a user wh"
"o has arrived at new installation of Tomcat, or you're an administrator who hasn't got his/her"
" setup quite right. Providing the latter is the case, please refer to the <a href=\"tomcat-doc"
"s\">Tomcat Documentation</a> for more detailed setup and administration information than is fo"
"und in the INSTALL file.</p>\r\n"
"\r\n"
"            <p><b>NOTE: For security reasons, using the administration webapp\r\n"
"            is restricted to users with role \"admin\". The manager webapp\r\n"
"            is restricted to users with role \"manager\".</b>\r\n"
"            Users are defined in <code>$CATALINA_HOME/conf/tomcat-users.xml</code>.</p>\r\n"
